        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In a
board meeting immediately following the Annual General Meeting of the
Shareholders of Alcon, Inc. on May 5, 2009, the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;)
of Alcon, Inc. re-elected Cary Rayment as its Non-Executive Chairman and
re-elected Francisco Casta&#241;er as its Vice-Chairman.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">At the
May 5, 2009 Board meeting, the Board approved an annual cash retainer of $85,000
(plus an additional $15,000 for the Audit Committee Chairman and an additional
$10,000 for the Compensation Committee Chairman , the Nominating/ Corporate
Governance Committee Chairman and the Independent Director Committee Chairman),
to each member of the Board, except for the Chief Executive Officer, for service
to Alcon, Inc. as a director for the period commencing at the Annual General
Meeting held on May 5, 2009 and ending at the next succeeding Annual General
Meeting.&#160;&#160;Additionally, upon the recommendation of the Compensation
Committee, the Board approved an award to each non-employee director of Alcon,
Inc. of 3,150 share-settled stock appreciation rights (&#8220;SSARs&#8221;) and 700
restricted share units (&#8220;RSUs&#8221;).&#160;&#160;The exercise price of a SSAR shall
be equal to the closing price of one common share of the Company, as reported on
the New York Stock Exchange on the date of grant, which is scheduled for Friday,
May 8, 2009 (the third trading day following the Annual General
Meeting).&#160;&#160;Both the SSARs and RSUs have a three-year vesting period
from the date of grant.&#160;&#160;A non-employee director is a director who is
neither a member of Nestl&#233;&#8217;s board of directors nor a full-time employee of
Nestl&#233; or Alcon.</font></div>
